  590: export async function syncInventory(locationId: string, organizationId: string): Promise<SyncResult> {
  591:   const start = Date.now()
  592:   const setup = await getClient(locationId)
  593:   if (!setup) return { ...emptySyncResult('inventory', 'full'), durationMs: Date.now() - start }
  594:   const { client } = setup
  595: 
  596:   const result = emptySyncResult('inventory', 'full')
  597:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
  598:   const logId = await createSyncLog(sb, locationId, 'inventory', 'full')
  599: 
  600:   try {
  601:     const dutchieItems = await client.fetchInventory({ includeLabResults: true, includeRoomQuantities: true })
  602:     result.fetched = dutchieItems.length
  603: 
  604:     // Build product_id lookup from dutchie_product_id
  605:     const productIdMap = await buildDutchieProductMap(sb, organizationId)
  606:     logger.info('Inventory product map built', { orgId: organizationId, mapSize: productIdMap.size, sampleKeys: [...productIdMap.keys()].slice(0, 5) })
  607: 
  608:     // Build room lookup by name
  609:     const roomMap = await buildRoomMap(sb, locationId)
  610: 
  611:     // Map all items
  612:     const mapped: Array<Record<string, unknown> & { external_package_id: string | null }> = []
  613:     for (const di of dutchieItems) {
  614:       try {
  615:         const item = mapInventoryItem(di, locationId)
  616:         item.product_id = productIdMap.get(di.productId) ?? null
  617:         // Room: try di.room first, then extract from roomQuantities array
  618:         const roomName = di.room
  619:           ?? (Array.isArray((di as Record<string, unknown>).roomQuantities)
  620:             ? ((di as Record<string, unknown>).roomQuantities as Array<Record<string, unknown>>)[0]?.room as string | null
  621:             : null)
  622:         item.room_id = roomName ? (roomMap.get(roomName.toLowerCase()) ?? null) : null
  623:         const row = { ...item, organization_id: organizationId } as Record<string, unknown> & { external_package_id: string | null }
  624:         mapped.push(row)
  625:       } catch (err) {
  626:         result.errored++
  627:         result.errors.push(`Inventory ${di.inventoryId}: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`)
  628:       }
  629:     }
  630: 
  631:     // Load existing inventory for this location
  632:     const { data: existing } = await (sb as any).from('inventory_items')
  633:       .select('id, external_package_id')
  634:       .eq('location_id', locationId)
  635:       .eq('is_active', true)
  636:       .limit(50000)
  637: 
  638:     const existingMap = new Map<string, string>()
  639:     for (const row of existing ?? []) {
  640:       if (row.external_package_id) existingMap.set(row.external_package_id, row.id)
  641:     }
  642: 
  643:     // Diff: new, update, soft-delete
  644:     const incomingIds = new Set<string>()
  645:     const toUpsert: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
  646: 
  647:     for (const item of mapped) {
  648:       if (item.external_package_id) incomingIds.add(item.external_package_id)
  649:       if (!item.product_id) { result.skipped++; continue }
  650:       toUpsert.push({ ...item, is_active: true })
  651:     }
  652: 
  653:     await batchUpsert(sb, 'inventory_items', toUpsert, 'location_id,external_package_id', result)
  654: 
  655:     // Soft-delete items missing from Dutchie
  656:     const toDeactivate = [...existingMap.entries()]
  657:       .filter(([extId]) => !incomingIds.has(extId))
  658:       .map(([, id]) => id)
  659: 
  660:     if (toDeactivate.length > 0) {
  661:       await softDeleteBatch(sb, 'inventory_items', toDeactivate)
  662:       result.updated += toDeactivate.length
  663:     }
  664: 
  665:   } catch (err) {
  666:     handleSyncError(err, result)
  667:   }
  668: 
  669:   if (result.fetched > 0) {
  670:     await updateSyncTimestamp(locationId, 'inventory', new Date(start))
  671:   }
  672: 
  673:   result.durationMs = Date.now() - start
  674:   await completeSyncLog(sb, logId, result)
  675:   logger.info('syncInventory complete', { locationId, ...result })
  676:   return result
  677: }
  678: 
  679: async function buildDutchieProductMap(sb: ReturnType<typeof Object>, orgId: string): Promise<Map<number, string>> {
  680:   // Paginate in chunks of 1000 (Supabase max-rows default)
  681:   const map = new Map<number, string>()
  682:   let offset = 0
  683:   const pageSize = 1000
  684:   while (true) {
  685:     const { data } = await (sb as any).from('products')
  686:       .select('id, dutchie_product_id')
  687:       .eq('organization_id', orgId)
  688:       .not('dutchie_product_id', 'is', null)
  689:       .order('dutchie_product_id', { ascending: true })
  690:       .range(offset, offset + pageSize - 1)
  691:     if (!data?.length) break
  692:     for (const p of data) map.set(p.dutchie_product_id, p.id)
  693:     if (data.length < pageSize) break
  694:     offset += pageSize
  695:   }
  696:   return map
  697: }
  698: 
  699: async function buildRoomMap(sb: ReturnType<typeof Object>, locationId: string): Promise<Map<string, string>> {
  700:   const { data } = await (sb as any).from('rooms')
  701:     .select('id, name')
  702:     .eq('location_id', locationId)
  703:     .eq('is_active', true)
  704: 
  705:   const map = new Map<string, string>()
  706:   for (const r of data ?? []) map.set(r.name?.toLowerCase(), r.id)
  707:   return map
  708: }
  709: 
  710: async function softDeleteBatch(sb: ReturnType<typeof Object>, table: string, ids: string[]): Promise<void> {
  711:   for (let i = 0; i < ids.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
  712:     const batch = ids.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE)
  713:     await (sb as any).from(table)
  714:       .update({ is_active: false, deactivated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
  715:       .in('id', batch)
  716:   }
  717: }

  771:               .upsert(subroomRows, { onConflict: 'room_id,name', ignoreDuplicates: false })
  772:           }
  773:           continue
  774:         }
  775: 
  776:         // Step 2: Check if room exists by external_id
  777:         const existingId = byExternalId.get(extId)
  778:         if (existingId) {
  779:           // Update existing
  780:           await (sb as any).from('rooms')

  947:         result.errors.push(`Terminal ${t.terminalId}: ${error.message}`)
  948:       } else {
  949:         result.updated++

  951:     }

  959: export async function syncTransactions(locationId: string, organizationId: string): Promise<SyncResult> {
  960:   const start = Date.now()
  961:   const setup = await getClient(locationId)
  962:   if (!setup) return { ...emptySyncResult('transactions', 'full'), durationMs: Date.now() - start }
  963:   const { client, config } = setup
  964: 
  965:   const result = emptySyncResult('transactions', 'full')
  966:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
  967:   const logId = await createSyncLog(sb, locationId, 'transactions', 'full')
  968: 
  969:   try {
  970:     // Fetch from last sync or last 90 days
  971:     const startMs = (config.lastSyncedTransactionsAt ?? new Date(Date.now() - 730 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)).getTime()
  972:     const endMs = Date.now()
  973:     const maxWindowMs = 55 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 // 55 days per chunk (under 1440hr limit)
  974: 
  975:     // Chunk into windows if range exceeds max
  976:     const dutchieTransactions: DutchieTransaction[] = []
  977:     let windowStart = startMs
  978:     while (windowStart < endMs) {
  979:       const windowEnd = Math.min(windowStart + maxWindowMs, endMs)
  980:       const startDate = new Date(windowStart).toISOString()
  981:       const endDate = new Date(windowEnd).toISOString()
  982:       logger.info('syncTransactions date range', { startDate: startDate.slice(0, 10), endDate: endDate.slice(0, 10) })
  983:       const chunk = await client.fetchTransactions({ startDate, endDate })
  984:       for (const t of chunk) dutchieTransactions.push(t)
  985:       windowStart = windowEnd
  986:     }
  987:     result.fetched = dutchieTransactions.length
  988: 
  989:     if (dutchieTransactions.length === 0) {
  990:       result.durationMs = Date.now() - start
  991:       await completeSyncLog(sb, logId, result)
  992:       return result
  993:     }
  994: 
  995:     // Build FK lookup maps (paginated to avoid 1000-row cap)
  996:     const customerMap = await buildPaginatedMap(sb, 'customers', 'dutchie_customer_id', 'id', { organization_id: organizationId })
  997:     const employeeMap = await buildPaginatedMap(sb, 'employees', 'dutchie_employee_id', 'id', { organization_id: organizationId })
  998: 
  999:     // Map all transactions
 1000:     const txRows: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
 1001:     const paymentRows: Array<{ dutchie_txn_id: string; payments: Array<{ payment_method: string; amount: number }> }> = []
 1002: 
 1003:     for (const dt of dutchieTransactions) {
 1004:       try {
 1005:         const { transaction, payments } = mapTransaction(dt, locationId)
 1006:         // Resolve FKs
 1007:         if (dt.customerId) {
 1008:           transaction.customer_id = customerMap.get(String(dt.customerId)) ?? null
 1009:         }
 1010:         if (dt.employeeId) {
 1011:           transaction.employee_id = employeeMap.get(String(dt.employeeId)) ?? null
 1012:         }
 1013:         txRows.push(transaction as unknown as Record<string, unknown>)
 1014:         paymentRows.push({ dutchie_txn_id: String(dt.transactionId), payments })
 1015:       } catch (err) {
 1016:         result.errored++
 1017:         result.errors.push(`Txn ${dt.transactionId}: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`)
 1018:       }
 1019:     }
 1020: 
 1021:     // Batch upsert transactions
 1022:     await batchUpsert(sb, 'transactions', txRows, 'location_id,dutchie_transaction_id', result)
 1023: 
 1024:     // Upsert payments â€” need to resolve transaction IDs first
 1025:     const txIdMap = await buildPaginatedMap(sb, 'transactions', 'dutchie_transaction_id', 'id', { location_id: locationId })
 1026: 
 1027:     const allPayments: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
 1028:     for (const pr of paymentRows) {
 1029:       const txId = txIdMap.get(pr.dutchie_txn_id)
 1030:       if (!txId) continue
 1031:       for (const p of pr.payments) {
 1032:         allPayments.push({ transaction_id: txId, ...p })
 1033:       }
 1034:     }
 1035: 
 1036:     if (allPayments.length > 0) {
 1037:       // Delete existing payments for these transactions and re-insert
 1038:       const txIds = [...new Set(allPayments.map(p => p.transaction_id as string))]
 1039:       for (let i = 0; i < txIds.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
 1040:         const batch = txIds.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE)
 1041:         await (sb as any).from('transaction_payments').delete().in('transaction_id', batch)
 1042:       }
 1043:       // Insert fresh payments
 1044:       for (let i = 0; i < allPayments.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {
 1045:         const batch = allPayments.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE)
 1046:         await (sb as any).from('transaction_payments').insert(batch)
 1047:       }
 1048:     }
 1049: 
 1050:     // Update customer aggregates (lifetime_spend, visit_count, last_visit_at)
 1051:     await updateCustomerAggregates(sb, organizationId)
 1052:   } catch (err) {
 1053:     handleSyncError(err, result)
 1054:   }
 1055: 
 1056:   if (result.fetched > 0) {
 1057:     await updateSyncTimestamp(locationId, 'transactions', new Date(start))
 1058:   }
 1059: 
 1060:   result.durationMs = Date.now() - start
 1061:   await completeSyncLog(sb, logId, result)
 1062:   logger.info('syncTransactions complete', { locationId, ...result })
 1063:   return result
 1064: }
 1065: 
 1066: async function buildPaginatedMap(
 1067:   sb: ReturnType<typeof Object>,
 1068:   table: string,
 1069:   keyCol: string,
 1070:   valueCol: string,
 1071:   filters: Record<string, string>,
 1072: ): Promise<Map<string, string>> {
 1073:   const map = new Map<string, string>()
 1074:   let offset = 0
 1075:   const pageSize = 1000
 1076:   while (true) {
 1077:     let query = (sb as any).from(table).select(`${valueCol}, ${keyCol}`).not(keyCol, 'is', null)
 1078:     for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(filters)) query = query.eq(k, v)
 1079:     const { data } = await query.order(keyCol, { ascending: true }).range(offset, offset + pageSize - 1)
 1080:     if (!data?.length) break
 1081:     for (const row of data) map.set(String(row[keyCol]), row[valueCol])
 1082:     if (data.length < pageSize) break
 1083:     offset += pageSize
 1084:   }
 1085:   return map
 1086: }
 1087: 
 1088: async function updateCustomerAggregates(sb: ReturnType<typeof Object>, orgId: string): Promise<void> {
 1089:   // Use a single SQL call to update all customer aggregates from transactions
 1090:   try {
 1091:     const { error } = await (sb as any).rpc('update_customer_aggregates_from_transactions', { org_id: orgId })
 1092:     if (error) logger.warn('Customer aggregate update skipped', { error: error.message })
 1093:   } catch {
 1094:     logger.warn('update_customer_aggregates_from_transactions RPC not found, skipping')
 1095:   }
 1096: }

 1117: const ENTITY_ENABLED_KEY: Record<EntityType, string> = {
 1118:   reference: 'isEnabled',
 1119:   rooms: 'syncRooms',
 1120:   employees: 'syncEmployees',
 1121:   products: 'syncProducts',
 1122:   customers: 'syncCustomers',
 1123:   inventory: 'syncInventory',
 1124:   transactions: 'syncInventory',
 1125: }
 1126: 
 1127: export async function syncLocation(
 1128:   locationId: string,
 1129:   organizationId: string,
 1130:   entityTypes?: EntityType[],
 1131: ): Promise<LocationSyncResult> {
 1132:   const start = Date.now()
 1133:   const config = await loadDutchieConfig(locationId)
 1134:   const locationName = config?.dutchieLocationName ?? locationId
 1135: 
 1136:   const results: SyncResult[] = []
 1137:   const typesToSync = entityTypes ?? SYNC_ORDER
 1138: 
 1139:   for (const entityType of SYNC_ORDER) {
 1140:     if (!typesToSync.includes(entityType)) continue
 1141:     const enabledKey = ENTITY_ENABLED_KEY[entityType] as keyof typeof config
 1142:     if (config && enabledKey !== 'isEnabled' && !(config as Record<string, unknown>)[enabledKey]) {
 1143:       logger.info('Skipping disabled entity sync', { locationId, entityType })
 1144:       continue
 1145:     }
 1146: 
 1147:     const syncResult = await SYNC_FN_MAP[entityType](locationId, organizationId)
 1148:     results.push(syncResult)
 1149:   }
 1150: 
 1151:   return {
 1152:     locationId,
 1153:     locationName,
 1154:     results,
 1155:     totalDurationMs: Date.now() - start,
 1156:   }
 1157: }

 1159: export async function syncAllLocations(organizationId: string): Promise<LocationSyncResult[]> {
 1160:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
 1161:   const { data: configs } = await (sb as any).from('dutchie_config')
 1162:     .select('location_id')
 1163:     .eq('is_enabled', true)
 1164: 
 1165:   if (!configs?.length) {
 1166:     logger.info('No enabled Dutchie configs found', { organizationId })
 1167:     return []
 1168:   }
 1169: 
 1170:   const results: LocationSyncResult[] = []
 1171: 
 1172:   // Sync org-wide entities once using the first location's API key
 1173:   const orgWideTypes = SYNC_ORDER.filter(t => ORG_WIDE_ENTITIES.has(t))
 1174:   const perLocationTypes = SYNC_ORDER.filter(t => !ORG_WIDE_ENTITIES.has(t))
 1175: 
 1176:   if (orgWideTypes.length > 0) {
 1177:     try {
 1178:       const orgResult = await syncLocation(configs[0].location_id, organizationId, orgWideTypes)
 1179:       results.push(orgResult)
 1180:     } catch (err) {
 1181:       logger.error('Org-wide sync failed', { error: String(err) })
 1182:     }
 1183:   }
 1184: 
 1185:   // Then sync per-location entities (rooms, inventory) for each location
 1186:   for (const config of configs) {
 1187:     try {
 1188:       const locationResult = await syncLocation(config.location_id, organizationId, perLocationTypes)
 1189:       results.push(locationResult)
 1190:     } catch (err) {
 1191:       logger.error('syncLocation failed', {
 1192:         locationId: config.location_id,
 1193:         error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
 1194:       })
 1195:     }
 1196:   }
 1197: 
 1198:   clearDutchieConfigCache()
 1199:   return results
 1200: }

 1206: function filterValid<T extends Record<string, unknown>>(
 1207:   records: T[],
 1208:   requiredField: string,
 1209:   result: SyncResult,
 1210: ): Record<string, unknown>[] {
 1211:   const valid: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
 1212:   for (const record of records) {
 1213:     if (record[requiredField] === undefined || record[requiredField] === null) {
 1214:       result.errored++
 1215:       result.errors.push(`Missing required field: ${requiredField}`)
 1216:       continue
 1217:     }
 1218:     valid.push(record)
 1219:   }
 1220:   return valid
 1221: }

 1223: function handleSyncError(err: unknown, result: SyncResult): void {
 1224:   const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)
 1225:   result.errored++
 1226:   result.errors.push(message)
 1227:   logger.error('Sync error', { error: message })
 1228: }

    1: import { logger } from '@/lib/utils/logger'
    2: import type {
    3:   DutchieEmployee, DutchieCustomer, DutchieProduct, DutchieInventoryItem,
    4:   DutchieRoom, DutchieBrand, DutchieStrain, DutchieVendor, DutchieCategory,
    5:   DutchieTag, DutchiePricingTier, DutchieTerminal, DutchieDiscount,
    6: } from './types'
    7: 
    8: const BASE_URL = 'https://api.pos.dutchie.com' // NO /v1 suffix
    9: const MAX_RETRIES = 4
   10: const REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 30000
   11: 
   12: export class DutchieClient {
   13:   private authHeader: string
   14: 
   15:   constructor(private apiKey: string) {
   16:     this.authHeader = `Basic ${Buffer.from(apiKey + ':').toString('base64')}`
   17:   }
   18: 
   19:   /**
   20:    * Core GET with rate limit retry + AbortSignal timeout.
   21:    * On 429: reads Retry-After header or uses exponential backoff 1sâ†’2sâ†’4sâ†’8s.
   22:    */
   23:   private async get<T>(path: string, params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean | undefined>): Promise<T> {
   24:     const url = new URL(`${BASE_URL}${path}`)
   25:     if (params) {
   26:       Object.entries(params).forEach(([k, v]) => {
   27:         if (v !== undefined) url.searchParams.set(k, String(v))
   28:       })
   29:     }
   30: 
   31:     let lastError: Error | null = null
   32:     for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= MAX_RETRIES; attempt++) {
   33:       try {
   34:         const start = Date.now()
   35:         const res = await fetch(url.toString(), {
   36:           method: 'GET',
   37:           headers: { Authorization: this.authHeader, Accept: 'application/json' },
   38:           signal: AbortSignal.timeout(REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS),
   39:         })
   40: 
   41:         if (res.status === 429) {
   42:           const retryAfter = res.headers.get('Retry-After')
   43:           const waitMs = retryAfter ? parseInt(retryAfter) * 1000 : Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000
   44:           logger.warn('Dutchie rate limited', { path, attempt, waitMs })
   45:           await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, waitMs))
   46:           continue
   47:         }
   48: 
   49:         if (!res.ok) {
   50:           const text = await res.text().catch(() => '')
   51:           throw new Error(`Dutchie API ${res.status}: ${text || res.statusText}`)
   52:         }
   53: 
   54:         const data = await res.json()
   55:         logger.info('Dutchie request', { path, status: res.status, ms: Date.now() - start })
   56:         return data as T
   57:       } catch (err) {
   58:         lastError = err instanceof Error ? err : new Error(String(err))
   59:         if (attempt < MAX_RETRIES && (lastError.name === 'AbortError' || lastError.message.includes('429'))) {
   60:           await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000))
   61:           continue
   62:         }
   63:         throw lastError
   64:       }
   65:     }
   66:     throw lastError || new Error('Max retries exceeded')
   67:   }
   68: 
   69:   /**
   70:    * Logs raw API response shape for debugging sync issues.
   71:    */
   72:   private logRawResponse(path: string, data: unknown): void {
   73:     const firstItem = Array.isArray(data) && data.length > 0 ? data[0] : data
   74:     const snippet = JSON.stringify(firstItem).slice(0, 2000)
   75:     logger.info('Dutchie raw response debug', { path, snippet })
   76:   }
   77: 
   78:   /**
   79:    * Unwraps responses that may be arrays or objects wrapping arrays.
   80:    */
   81:   private unwrap<T>(data: unknown): T[] {
   82:     if (Array.isArray(data)) return data
   83:     if (typeof data === 'object' && data !== null) {
   84:       const vals = Object.values(data)
   85:       const arr = vals.find(v => Array.isArray(v))
   86:       if (arr) return arr as T[]
   87:     }
   88:     logger.warn('Dutchie unwrap: unexpected response shape', {
   89:       type: typeof data,
   90:       keys: typeof data === 'object' && data !== null ? Object.keys(data).slice(0, 10) : [],
   91:     })
   92:     return []
   93:   }
   94: 
   95:   /**
   96:    * Auto-paginates offset/limit endpoints (products, inventory).
   97:    */
   98:   private async fetchAllOffset<T>(
   99:     path: string,
  100:     params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean | undefined>,
  101:     pageSize = 100,
  102:   ): Promise<T[]> {
  103:     const all: T[] = []
  104:     let offset = 0
  105: 
  106:     while (true) {
  107:       const data = await this.get<unknown>(path, { ...params, offset, limit: pageSize })
  108:       if (offset === 0) this.logRawResponse(path, data)
  109:       const items = this.unwrap<T>(data)
  110:       if (items.length === 0) break
  111:       for (const item of items) all.push(item)
  112:       if (items.length < pageSize) break
  113:       offset += items.length
  114:     }
  115: 
  116:     logger.info('Dutchie paginated fetch complete', { path, total: all.length })
  117:     return all
  118:   }
  119: 
  120:   /**
  121:    * Auto-paginates PageNumber/PageSize endpoints (customers-paginated).
  122:    */
  123:   private async fetchAllPaged<T>(
  124:     path: string,
  125:     params?: Record<string, string | number | boolean | undefined>,
  126:     pageSize = 100,
  127:   ): Promise<T[]> {
  128:     const all: T[] = []
  129:     let page = 1
  130: 
  131:     while (true) {
  132:       const data = await this.get<unknown>(path, { ...params, PageNumber: page, PageSize: pageSize })
  133:       const items = this.unwrap<T>(data)
  134:       if (items.length === 0) break
  135:       for (const item of items) all.push(item)
  136:       if (items.length < pageSize) break
  137:       page++
  138:     }
  139: 
  140:     logger.info('Dutchie paged fetch complete', { path, total: all.length })
  141:     return all
  142:   }

    6: /**
    7:  * GET /api/dutchie/jobs â€” List recent sync jobs with optional location filter
    8:  */
    9: 
   10: export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
   11:   try {
   12:     await requireSession()
   13:     const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
   14: 
   15:     const locationId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('location_id')
   16:     const limit = Math.min(parseInt(request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('limit') ?? '50'), 100)
   17: 
   18:     // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   19:     let query = (sb as any).from('dutchie_sync_jobs')
   20:       .select('*')
   21:       .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
   22:       .limit(limit)
   23: 
   24:     if (locationId) {
   25:       query = query.eq('location_id', locationId)
   26:     }
   27: 
   28:     const { data, error } = await query
   29: 
   30:     if (error) {
   31:       return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
   32:     }
   33: 
   34:     return NextResponse.json({ jobs: data ?? [] })
   35:   } catch (err) {
   36:     if (err && typeof err === 'object' && 'code' in err) {
   37:       const a = err as { code: string; statusCode?: number }
   38:       if (a.code === 'UNAUTHORIZED') return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Auth required' }, { status: 401 })
   39:     }
   40:     logger.error('Dutchie jobs GET error', { error: String(err) })
   41:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Server error' }, { status: 500 })
   42:   }
   43: }

    1: CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_sale_transaction(
    2:   p_location_id UUID,
    3:   p_employee_id UUID,
    4:   p_register_id UUID,
    5:   p_customer_id UUID,
    6:   p_cash_drawer_id UUID,
    7:   p_is_medical BOOLEAN,
    8:   p_subtotal NUMERIC(12,2),
    9:   p_discount_total NUMERIC(12,2),
   10:   p_tax_total NUMERIC(12,2),
   11:   p_total NUMERIC(12,2),
   12:   p_lines JSONB,
   13:   p_payments JSONB,
   14:   p_taxes JSONB,
   15:   p_discounts JSONB,
   16:   p_loyalty_points INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
   17:   p_organization_id UUID DEFAULT NULL
   18: ) RETURNS JSONB
   19: LANGUAGE plpgsql
   20: AS $$
   21: DECLARE
   22:   v_tx_id UUID;
   23:   v_tx_number INTEGER;
   24:   v_line JSONB;
   25:   v_payment JSONB;
   26:   v_tax JSONB;
   27:   v_discount JSONB;
   28:   v_rows_affected INTEGER;
   29:   v_org_id UUID;
   30:   v_balance_after INTEGER;
   31: BEGIN
   32:   -- Resolve organization_id from location if not provided
   33:   IF p_organization_id IS NULL THEN
   34:     SELECT organization_id INTO v_org_id FROM locations WHERE id = p_location_id;
   35:   ELSE
   36:     v_org_id := p_organization_id;
   37:   END IF;
   38: 
   39:   -- Generate next transaction number for this location (with lock)
   40:   SELECT COALESCE(MAX(transaction_number), 0) + 1
   41:     INTO v_tx_number
   42:     FROM transactions
   43:     WHERE location_id = p_location_id
   44:     FOR UPDATE;
   45: 
   46:   -- Verify cash drawer is open
   47:   PERFORM 1 FROM cash_drawers
   48:     WHERE id = p_cash_drawer_id AND status = 'open'
   49:     FOR UPDATE;
   50:   IF NOT FOUND THEN
   51:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Cash drawer is not open';
   52:   END IF;
   53: 
   54:   -- Insert transaction header
   55:   INSERT INTO transactions (
   56:     location_id, employee_id, register_id, customer_id,
   57:     transaction_number, transaction_type, status,
   58:     is_medical, subtotal, discount_amount, tax_amount, total
   59:   ) VALUES (
   60:     p_location_id, p_employee_id, p_register_id, p_customer_id,
   61:     v_tx_number, 'sale', 'completed',
   62:     p_is_medical, p_subtotal, p_discount_total, p_tax_total, p_total
   63:   ) RETURNING id INTO v_tx_id;
   64: 
   65:   -- Insert lines and decrement inventory
   66:   FOR v_line IN SELECT * FROM jsonb_array_elements(p_lines)
   67:   LOOP
   68:     INSERT INTO transaction_lines (
   69:       transaction_id, product_id, inventory_item_id,
   70:       product_name, category_name, quantity, unit_price,
   71:       discount_amount, tax_amount, line_total,
   72:       is_cannabis, is_medical, weight_grams,
   73:       flower_equivalent_grams, biotrack_barcode
   74:     ) VALUES (
   75:       v_tx_id,
   76:       (v_line->>'product_id')::UUID,
   77:       (v_line->>'inventory_item_id')::UUID,
   78:       v_line->>'product_name',
   79:       v_line->>'category_name',
   80:       (v_line->>'quantity')::INTEGER,
   81:       (v_line->>'unit_price')::NUMERIC(12,2),
   82:       (v_line->>'discount_amount')::NUMERIC(12,2),
   83:       (v_line->>'tax_amount')::NUMERIC(12,2),
   84:       (v_line->>'line_total')::NUMERIC(12,2),
   85:       COALESCE((v_line->>'is_cannabis')::BOOLEAN, true),
   86:       p_is_medical,
   87:       (v_line->>'weight_grams')::NUMERIC(8,3),
   88:       (v_line->>'flower_equivalent_grams')::NUMERIC(8,3),
   89:       v_line->>'biotrack_barcode'
   90:     );
   91: 
   92:     -- Decrement inventory
   93:     IF v_line->>'inventory_item_id' IS NOT NULL THEN
   94:       UPDATE inventory_items
   95:         SET quantity = quantity - (v_line->>'quantity')::INTEGER,
   96:             updated_at = NOW()
   97:         WHERE id = (v_line->>'inventory_item_id')::UUID
   98:           AND quantity >= (v_line->>'quantity')::INTEGER;
   99: 
  100:       GET DIAGNOSTICS v_rows_affected = ROW_COUNT;
  101:       IF v_rows_affected = 0 THEN
  102:         RAISE EXCEPTION 'Insufficient inventory for product %', v_line->>'product_name';
  103:       END IF;
  104:     END IF;
  105:   END LOOP;
  106: 
  107:   -- Insert payments
  108:   FOR v_payment IN SELECT * FROM jsonb_array_elements(p_payments)
  109:   LOOP
  110:     INSERT INTO transaction_payments (
  111:       transaction_id, payment_method, amount, tendered, change_given, reference_number
  112:     ) VALUES (
  113:       v_tx_id,
  114:       v_payment->>'payment_method',
  115:       (v_payment->>'amount')::NUMERIC(12,2),
  116:       (v_payment->>'tendered')::NUMERIC(12,2),
  117:       (v_payment->>'change_given')::NUMERIC(12,2),
  118:       v_payment->>'reference_number'
  119:     );
  120:   END LOOP;
  121: 
  122:   -- Insert taxes
  123:   FOR v_tax IN SELECT * FROM jsonb_array_elements(p_taxes)
  124:   LOOP
  125:     INSERT INTO transaction_taxes (
  126:       transaction_id, tax_name, tax_rate, taxable_amount, tax_amount, is_excise
  127:     ) VALUES (
  128:       v_tx_id,
  129:       v_tax->>'tax_name',
  130:       (v_tax->>'tax_rate')::NUMERIC(8,6),
  131:       (v_tax->>'taxable_amount')::NUMERIC(12,2),
  132:       (v_tax->>'tax_amount')::NUMERIC(12,2),
  133:       COALESCE((v_tax->>'is_excise')::BOOLEAN, false)
  134:     );
  135:   END LOOP;
  136: 
  137:   -- Insert discounts
  138:   FOR v_discount IN SELECT * FROM jsonb_array_elements(p_discounts)
  139:   LOOP
  140:     INSERT INTO transaction_discounts (
  141:       transaction_id, discount_id, discount_name, discount_amount
  142:     ) VALUES (
  143:       v_tx_id,
  144:       NULLIF(v_discount->>'discount_id', '')::UUID,
  145:       v_discount->>'discount_name',
  146:       (v_discount->>'discount_amount')::NUMERIC(12,2)
  147:     );
  148:   END LOOP;
  149: 
  150:   -- Update customer stats
  151:   IF p_customer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
  152:     UPDATE customers
  153:       SET last_visit_at = NOW(),
  154:           lifetime_spend = lifetime_spend + p_total,
  155:           visit_count = visit_count + 1,
  156:           updated_at = NOW()
  157:       WHERE id = p_customer_id;
  158: 
  159:     -- Award loyalty points
  160:     IF p_loyalty_points > 0 THEN
  161:       UPDATE loyalty_balances
  162:         SET current_points = current_points + p_loyalty_points,
  163:             lifetime_points = lifetime_points + p_loyalty_points,
  164:             updated_at = NOW()
  165:         WHERE customer_id = p_customer_id
  166:         RETURNING current_points INTO v_balance_after;
  167: 
  168:       IF v_balance_after IS NOT NULL THEN
  169:         INSERT INTO loyalty_transactions (
  170:           customer_id, organization_id, points_change,
  171:           balance_after, reason, transaction_id
  172:         ) VALUES (
  173:           p_customer_id, v_org_id, p_loyalty_points,
  174:           v_balance_after, 'earn', v_tx_id
  175:         );
  176:       END IF;
  177:     END IF;
  178:   END IF;
  179: 
  180:   -- Update cash drawer
  181:   UPDATE cash_drawers
  182:     SET total_sales = total_sales + p_total,
  183:         updated_at = NOW()
  184:     WHERE id = p_cash_drawer_id;
  185: 
  186:   -- Audit log
  187:   INSERT INTO audit_log (
  188:     organization_id, location_id, employee_id,
  189:     entity_type, event_type, entity_id
  190:   ) VALUES (
  191:     v_org_id, p_location_id, p_employee_id,
  192:     'transaction', 'create', v_tx_id::TEXT
  193:   );
  194: 
  195:   RETURN jsonb_build_object(
  196:     'transaction_id', v_tx_id,
  197:     'transaction_number', v_tx_number
  198:   );
  199: END;
  200: $$;
===== supabase/migrations/20260330180000_void_return_functions.sql 1..285 =====
    1: -- Void a completed same-day transaction
    2: CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION void_transaction(
    3:   p_transaction_id UUID,
    4:   p_employee_id UUID,
    5:   p_void_reason TEXT,
    6:   p_cash_drawer_id UUID
    7: ) RETURNS JSONB
    8: LANGUAGE plpgsql
    9: AS $$
   10: DECLARE
   11:   v_tx RECORD;
   12:   v_line RECORD;
   13:   v_org_id UUID;
   14:   v_earned_points INTEGER;
   15:   v_rows INTEGER;
   16: BEGIN
   17:   -- Load and lock the transaction
   18:   SELECT * INTO v_tx FROM transactions WHERE id = p_transaction_id FOR UPDATE;
   19:   IF NOT FOUND THEN
   20:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Transaction not found';
   21:   END IF;
   22:   IF v_tx.status != 'completed' THEN
   23:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Transaction status is %, expected completed', v_tx.status;
   24:   END IF;
   25:   IF v_tx.created_at::date != CURRENT_DATE THEN
   26:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Can only void same-day transactions';
   27:   END IF;
   28: 
   29:   SELECT organization_id INTO v_org_id FROM locations WHERE id = v_tx.location_id;
   30: 
   31:   -- Mark as voided
   32:   UPDATE transactions
   33:     SET status = 'voided',
   34:         voided_by = p_employee_id,
   35:         voided_at = NOW(),
   36:         void_reason = p_void_reason,
   37:         updated_at = NOW()
   38:     WHERE id = p_transaction_id;
   39: 
   40:   -- Restore inventory for each line
   41:   FOR v_line IN SELECT * FROM transaction_lines WHERE transaction_id = p_transaction_id
   42:   LOOP
   43:     IF v_line.inventory_item_id IS NOT NULL THEN
   44:       UPDATE inventory_items
   45:         SET quantity = quantity + v_line.quantity,
   46:             updated_at = NOW()
   47:         WHERE id = v_line.inventory_item_id;
   48:     END IF;
   49:   END LOOP;
   50: 
   51:   -- Reverse customer stats
   52:   IF v_tx.customer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
   53:     UPDATE customers
   54:       SET lifetime_spend = GREATEST(0, lifetime_spend - v_tx.total),
   55:           visit_count = GREATEST(0, visit_count - 1),
   56:           updated_at = NOW()
   57:       WHERE id = v_tx.customer_id;
   58: 
   59:     -- Reverse loyalty points
   60:     SELECT COALESCE(SUM(points_change), 0) INTO v_earned_points
   61:       FROM loyalty_transactions
   62:       WHERE transaction_id = p_transaction_id AND reason = 'earn';
   63: 
   64:     IF v_earned_points > 0 THEN
   65:       UPDATE loyalty_balances
   66:         SET current_points = GREATEST(0, current_points - v_earned_points),
   67:             lifetime_points = GREATEST(0, lifetime_points - v_earned_points),
   68:             updated_at = NOW()
   69:         WHERE customer_id = v_tx.customer_id;
   70: 
   71:       INSERT INTO loyalty_transactions (
   72:         customer_id, organization_id, points_change,
   73:         balance_after, reason, transaction_id
   74:       ) VALUES (
   75:         v_tx.customer_id, v_org_id, -v_earned_points,
   76:         (SELECT current_points FROM loyalty_balances WHERE customer_id = v_tx.customer_id),
   77:         'void_reversal', p_transaction_id
   78:       );
   79:     END IF;
   80:   END IF;
   81: 
   82:   -- Reverse cash drawer
   83:   IF p_cash_drawer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
   84:     UPDATE cash_drawers
   85:       SET total_sales = GREATEST(0, total_sales - v_tx.total),
   86:           updated_at = NOW()
   87:       WHERE id = p_cash_drawer_id;
   88:   END IF;
   89: 
   90:   -- Audit log
   91:   INSERT INTO audit_log (
   92:     organization_id, location_id, employee_id,
   93:     entity_type, event_type, entity_id, metadata
   94:   ) VALUES (
   95:     v_org_id, v_tx.location_id, p_employee_id,
   96:     'transaction', 'void', p_transaction_id::TEXT,
   97:     jsonb_build_object('void_reason', p_void_reason, 'original_total', v_tx.total)
   98:   );
   99: 
  100:   RETURN jsonb_build_object(
  101:     'transaction_id', p_transaction_id,
  102:     'transaction_number', v_tx.transaction_number,
  103:     'voided_total', v_tx.total,
  104:     'items_restored', (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM transaction_lines WHERE transaction_id = p_transaction_id AND inventory_item_id IS NOT NULL)
  105:   );
  106: END;
  107: $$;
  108: 
  109: -- Process a return (full or partial)
  110: CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_return_transaction(
  111:   p_organization_id UUID,
  112:   p_location_id UUID,
  113:   p_employee_id UUID,
  114:   p_register_id UUID,
  115:   p_customer_id UUID,
  116:   p_cash_drawer_id UUID,
  117:   p_original_transaction_id UUID,
  118:   p_return_reason TEXT,
  119:   p_return_lines JSONB,
  120:   p_refund_amount NUMERIC(12,2)
  121: ) RETURNS JSONB
  122: LANGUAGE plpgsql
  123: AS $$
  124: DECLARE
  125:   v_orig RECORD;
  126:   v_tx_id UUID;
  127:   v_tx_number INTEGER;
  128:   v_rline JSONB;
  129:   v_orig_line RECORD;
  130:   v_already_returned INTEGER;
  131:   v_earned_points INTEGER;
  132:   v_proportional_points INTEGER;
  133:   v_org_id UUID;
  134: BEGIN
  135:   v_org_id := p_organization_id;
  136: 
  137:   -- Load and verify original transaction
  138:   SELECT * INTO v_orig FROM transactions WHERE id = p_original_transaction_id;
  139:   IF NOT FOUND THEN
  140:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Original transaction not found';
  141:   END IF;
  142:   IF v_orig.status != 'completed' THEN
  143:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Original transaction status is %, expected completed', v_orig.status;
  144:   END IF;
  145:   IF v_orig.created_at < NOW() - INTERVAL '14 days' THEN
  146:     RAISE EXCEPTION 'Return window expired (14 days)';
  147:   END IF;
  148: 
  149:   -- Generate next transaction number
  150:   SELECT COALESCE(MAX(transaction_number), 0) + 1
  151:     INTO v_tx_number
  152:     FROM transactions
  153:     WHERE location_id = p_location_id
  154:     FOR UPDATE;
  155: 
  156:   -- Create the return transaction
  157:   INSERT INTO transactions (
  158:     location_id, employee_id, register_id, customer_id,
  159:     transaction_number, transaction_type, status,
  160:     original_transaction_id, notes,
  161:     is_medical, subtotal, discount_amount, tax_amount, total
  162:   ) VALUES (
  163:     p_location_id, p_employee_id, p_register_id, p_customer_id,
  164:     v_tx_number, 'return', 'completed',
  165:     p_original_transaction_id, p_return_reason,
  166:     v_orig.is_medical, -p_refund_amount, 0, 0, -p_refund_amount
  167:   ) RETURNING id INTO v_tx_id;
  168: 
  169:   -- Process each return line
  170:   FOR v_rline IN SELECT * FROM jsonb_array_elements(p_return_lines)
  171:   LOOP
  172:     -- Load original line
  173:     SELECT * INTO v_orig_line
  174:       FROM transaction_lines
  175:       WHERE id = (v_rline->>'transaction_line_id')::UUID;
  176: 
  177:     IF NOT FOUND THEN
  178:       RAISE EXCEPTION 'Original transaction line not found: %', v_rline->>'transaction_line_id';
  179:     END IF;
  180: 
  181:     -- Check for double-return: count already returned qty for this line
  182:     SELECT COALESCE(SUM(ABS(tl.quantity)), 0) INTO v_already_returned
  183:       FROM transaction_lines tl
  184:       JOIN transactions t ON t.id = tl.transaction_id
  185:       WHERE t.original_transaction_id = p_original_transaction_id
  186:         AND t.transaction_type = 'return'
  187:         AND t.status = 'completed'
  188:         AND tl.product_id = v_orig_line.product_id
  189:         AND tl.inventory_item_id = v_orig_line.inventory_item_id;
  190: 
  191:     IF v_already_returned + (v_rline->>'quantity')::INTEGER > v_orig_line.quantity THEN
  192:       RAISE EXCEPTION 'Return quantity exceeds available for product %', v_orig_line.product_name;
  193:     END IF;
  194: 
  195:     -- Insert return line (negative quantity)
  196:     INSERT INTO transaction_lines (
  197:       transaction_id, product_id, inventory_item_id,
  198:       product_name, category_name, quantity, unit_price,
  199:       discount_amount, tax_amount, line_total,
  200:       is_cannabis, is_medical, weight_grams, biotrack_barcode
  201:     ) VALUES (
  202:       v_tx_id, v_orig_line.product_id, v_orig_line.inventory_item_id,
  203:       v_orig_line.product_name, v_orig_line.category_name,
  204:       -(v_rline->>'quantity')::INTEGER, v_orig_line.unit_price,
  205:       0, 0,
  206:       -(v_orig_line.line_total / v_orig_line.quantity * (v_rline->>'quantity')::INTEGER),
  207:       v_orig_line.is_cannabis, v_orig_line.is_medical,
  208:       v_orig_line.weight_grams, v_orig_line.biotrack_barcode
  209:     );
  210: 
  211:     -- Restore inventory if flagged
  212:     IF COALESCE((v_rline->>'restore_to_inventory')::BOOLEAN, true) AND v_orig_line.inventory_item_id IS NOT NULL THEN
  213:       UPDATE inventory_items
  214:         SET quantity = quantity + (v_rline->>'quantity')::INTEGER,
  215:             updated_at = NOW()
  216:         WHERE id = v_orig_line.inventory_item_id;
  217:     END IF;
  218:   END LOOP;
  219: 
  220:   -- Refund payment
  221:   INSERT INTO transaction_payments (
  222:     transaction_id, payment_method, amount, tendered, change_given
  223:   ) VALUES (
  224:     v_tx_id, 'cash', -p_refund_amount, NULL, NULL
  225:   );
  226: 
  227:   -- Reverse customer stats
  228:   IF p_customer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
  229:     UPDATE customers
  230:       SET lifetime_spend = GREATEST(0, lifetime_spend - p_refund_amount),
  231:           updated_at = NOW()
  232:       WHERE id = p_customer_id;
  233: 
  234:     -- Reverse proportional loyalty points
  235:     IF v_orig.total > 0 THEN
  236:       SELECT COALESCE(SUM(points_change), 0) INTO v_earned_points
  237:         FROM loyalty_transactions
  238:         WHERE transaction_id = p_original_transaction_id AND reason = 'earn';
  239: 
  240:       v_proportional_points := ROUND(v_earned_points * (p_refund_amount / v_orig.total));
  241: 
  242:       IF v_proportional_points > 0 THEN
  243:         UPDATE loyalty_balances
  244:           SET current_points = GREATEST(0, current_points - v_proportional_points),
  245:               lifetime_points = GREATEST(0, lifetime_points - v_proportional_points),
  246:               updated_at = NOW()
  247:           WHERE customer_id = p_customer_id;
  248: 
  249:         INSERT INTO loyalty_transactions (
  250:           customer_id, organization_id, points_change,
  251:           balance_after, reason, transaction_id
  252:         ) VALUES (
  253:           p_customer_id, v_org_id, -v_proportional_points,
  254:           (SELECT current_points FROM loyalty_balances WHERE customer_id = p_customer_id),
  255:           'return_reversal', v_tx_id
  256:         );
  257:       END IF;
  258:     END IF;
  259:   END IF;
  260: 
  261:   -- Update cash drawer
  262:   IF p_cash_drawer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
  263:     UPDATE cash_drawers
  264:       SET total_returns = total_returns + p_refund_amount,
  265:           updated_at = NOW()
  266:       WHERE id = p_cash_drawer_id;
  267:   END IF;
  268: 
  269:   -- Audit log
  270:   INSERT INTO audit_log (
  271:     organization_id, location_id, employee_id,
  272:     entity_type, event_type, entity_id, metadata
  273:   ) VALUES (
  274:     v_org_id, p_location_id, p_employee_id,
  275:     'transaction', 'return', v_tx_id::TEXT,
  276:     jsonb_build_object('original_transaction_id', p_original_transaction_id, 'refund_amount', p_refund_amount, 'return_reason', p_return_reason)
  277:   );
  278: 
  279:   RETURN jsonb_build_object(
  280:     'transaction_id', v_tx_id,
  281:     'transaction_number', v_tx_number,
  282:     'refund_amount', p_refund_amount,
  283:     'original_transaction_id', p_original_transaction_id
  284:   );
  285: END;
===== src/app/api/customers/[id]/loyalty/adjust/route.ts 1..150 =====
    1: import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
    2: import { z } from 'zod/v4'
    3: import { requireSession } from '@/lib/auth/session'
    4: import { createSupabaseServerClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server'
    5: import { logger } from '@/lib/utils/logger'
    6: 
    7: const AdjustSchema = z.object({
    8:   points: z.number().int(),
    9:   reason: z.string().min(1).max(500),
   10:   notes: z.string().max(1000).optional(),
   11: })
   12: 
   13: export async function POST(
   14:   request: NextRequest,
   15:   { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> },
   16: ) {
   17:   try {
   18:     const session = await requireSession()
   19:     const { id: customerId } = await params
   20:     const body = await request.json()
   21:     const parsed = AdjustSchema.safeParse(body)
   22: 
   23:     if (!parsed.success) {
   24:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid input', details: parsed.error.issues }, { status: 400 })
   25:     }
   26: 
   27:     const { points, reason, notes } = parsed.data
   28:     const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
   29: 
   30:     // Fetch or create loyalty balance
   31:     const { data: existing, error: fetchError } = await sb
   32:       .from('loyalty_balances')
   33:       .select('id, current_points, lifetime_points')
   34:       .eq('customer_id', customerId)
   35:       .eq('organization_id', session.organizationId)
   36:       .maybeSingle()
   37: 
   38:     if (fetchError) {
   39:       logger.error('Loyalty balance fetch failed', { error: fetchError.message, customerId })
   40:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch loyalty balance' }, { status: 500 })
   41:     }
   42: 
   43:     let balanceId: string
   44:     let currentPoints: number
   45:     let lifetimePoints: number
   46: 
   47:     if (!existing) {
   48:       // Create a new loyalty balance record
   49:       const { data: created, error: createError } = await sb
   50:         .from('loyalty_balances')
   51:         .insert({
   52:           customer_id: customerId,
   53:           organization_id: session.organizationId,
   54:           current_points: 0,
   55:           lifetime_points: 0,
   56:         })
   57:         .select('id, current_points, lifetime_points')
   58:         .single()
   59: 
   60:       if (createError || !created) {
   61:         logger.error('Loyalty balance creation failed', { error: createError?.message, customerId })
   62:         return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to create loyalty balance' }, { status: 500 })
   63:       }
   64: 
   65:       balanceId = created.id
   66:       currentPoints = created.current_points
   67:       lifetimePoints = created.lifetime_points
   68:     } else {
   69:       balanceId = existing.id
   70:       currentPoints = existing.current_points
   71:       lifetimePoints = existing.lifetime_points
   72:     }
   73: 
   74:     const newCurrentPoints = currentPoints + points
   75:     const newLifetimePoints = lifetimePoints + Math.max(0, points)
   76: 
   77:     if (newCurrentPoints < 0) {
   78:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Adjustment would result in negative balance' }, { status: 400 })
   79:     }
   80: 
   81:     // Update the balance
   82:     const { error: updateError } = await sb
   83:       .from('loyalty_balances')
   84:       .update({
   85:         current_points: newCurrentPoints,
   86:         lifetime_points: newLifetimePoints,
   87:       })
   88:       .eq('id', balanceId)
   89: 
   90:     if (updateError) {
   91:       logger.error('Loyalty balance update failed', { error: updateError.message, customerId })
   92:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to update loyalty balance' }, { status: 500 })
   93:     }
   94: 
   95:     // Insert loyalty transaction record
   96:     const { error: txnError } = await sb
   97:       .from('loyalty_transactions')
   98:       .insert({
   99:         customer_id: customerId,
  100:         organization_id: session.organizationId,
  101:         points_change: points,
  102:         balance_after: newCurrentPoints,
  103:         reason,
  104:         notes: notes ?? null,
  105:         created_by: session.employeeId,
  106:       })
  107: 
  108:     if (txnError) {
  109:       logger.error('Loyalty transaction insert failed', { error: txnError.message, customerId })
  110:       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to record loyalty transaction' }, { status: 500 })
  111:     }
  112: 
  113:     // Audit log
  114:     const { error: auditError } = await sb
  115:       .from('audit_log')
  116:       .insert({
  117:         organization_id: session.organizationId,
  118:         entity_type: 'loyalty_balance',
  119:         entity_id: balanceId,
  120:         event_type: 'adjust',
  121:         details: {
  122:           customer_id: customerId,
  123:           points_change: points,
  124:           balance_before: currentPoints,
  125:           balance_after: newCurrentPoints,
  126:           reason,
  127:           notes: notes ?? null,
  128:         },
  129:         performed_by: session.employeeId,
  130:       })
  131: 
  132:     if (auditError) {
  133:       logger.error('Loyalty adjust audit log failed', { error: auditError.message })
  134:     }
  135: 
  136:     return NextResponse.json({ success: true, new_balance: newCurrentPoints })
  137:   } catch (err) {
  138:     if (err && typeof err === 'object' && 'code' in err) {
  139:       const appErr = err as { code: string; message: string; statusCode?: number }
  140:       if (appErr.code === 'UNAUTHORIZED') return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Authentication required' }, { status: 401 })
  141:       return NextResponse.json({ error: appErr.message }, { status: appErr.statusCode ?? 500 })
  142:     }
  143:     logger.error('Loyalty adjust error', { error: String(err) })
  144:     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Server error' }, { status: 500 })
  145:   }
  146: }

    5: export async function adjustLoyaltyPoints(
    6:   customerId: string, points: number, reasonId: string, notes: string, employeeId: string, orgId: string,
    7: ) {
    8:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
    9: 
   10:   // Verify reason
   11:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   12:   const { data: reason } = await (sb.from('loyalty_adjustment_reasons') as any).select('*').eq('id', reasonId).eq('is_active', true).single()
   13:   if (!reason) throw new AppError('INVALID_REASON', 'Adjustment reason not found', undefined, 400)
   14: 
   15:   // Load current balance
   16:   const { data: balance } = await sb.from('loyalty_balances').select('current_points').eq('customer_id', customerId).single()
   17:   if (!balance) throw new AppError('NO_BALANCE', 'Customer has no loyalty balance', undefined, 400)
   18: 
   19:   const newBalance = balance.current_points + points
   20:   if (newBalance < 0) throw new AppError('INSUFFICIENT_POINTS', 'Adjustment would make balance negative', undefined, 400)
   21: 
   22:   await sb.from('loyalty_balances').update({ current_points: newBalance, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() }).eq('customer_id', customerId)
   23: 
   24:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   25:   await (sb.from('loyalty_transactions') as any).insert({
   26:     customer_id: customerId, organization_id: orgId, points_change: points,
   27:     balance_after: newBalance, reason: 'manual_adjust', adjustment_reason_id: reasonId,
   28:     created_by: employeeId,
   29:   })
   30: 
   31:   // Audit
   32:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   33:   await sb.from('audit_log').insert({
   34:     organization_id: orgId, employee_id: employeeId, entity_type: 'loyalty',
   35:     event_type: 'adjust', entity_id: customerId, metadata: { points, reason: reason.name, notes, new_balance: newBalance },
   36:   } as any)
   37: 
   38:   logger.info('Loyalty adjusted', { customerId, points, newBalance })
   39: }

   26: export async function createReferral(referrerId: string, refereeId: string, orgId: string) {
   27:   if (referrerId === refereeId) throw new AppError('SELF_REFERRAL', 'Cannot refer yourself', undefined, 400)
   28: 
   29:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
   30: 
   31:   // Check duplicate
   32:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any

   39:   }).select().single()
   40:

   45: export async function checkAndCompleteReferral(refereeCustomerId: string, transactionTotal: number, orgId: string) {
   46:   const sb = await createSupabaseServerClient()
   47: 
   48:   const config = await getReferralConfig(orgId)
   49:   if (!config) return null
   50: 
   51:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   52:   const { data: pending } = await (sb.from('referral_tracking') as any).select('*').eq('referee_customer_id', refereeCustomerId).eq('status', 'pending').maybeSingle()
   53:   if (!pending) return null
   54: 
   55:   if (transactionTotal < (config.min_purchase_amount ?? 0)) return null
   56: 
   57:   // Complete referral
   58:   // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   59:   await (sb.from('referral_tracking') as any).update({ status: 'completed', completed_at: new Date().toISOString(), referrer_rewarded: true, referee_rewarded: true }).eq('id', pending.id)
   60: 
   61:   // Award points to referrer
   62:   if (config.referrer_reward_points > 0) {
   63:     await sb.from('loyalty_balances').update({
   64:       current_points: (await sb.from('loyalty_balances').select('current_points').eq('customer_id', pending.referrer_customer_id).single()).data?.current_points + config.referrer_reward_points,
   65:     } as Record<string, unknown>).eq('customer_id', pending.referrer_customer_id)
   66: 
   67:     // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   68:     await (sb.from('loyalty_transactions') as any).insert({
   69:       customer_id: pending.referrer_customer_id, organization_id: orgId,
   70:       points_change: config.referrer_reward_points, balance_after: 0, reason: 'referral_bonus',
   71:     })
   72:   }
   73: 
   74:   // Award points to referee
   75:   if (config.referee_reward_points > 0) {
   76:     await sb.from('loyalty_balances').update({
   77:       current_points: (await sb.from('loyalty_balances').select('current_points').eq('customer_id', refereeCustomerId).single()).data?.current_points + config.referee_reward_points,
   78:     } as Record<string, unknown>).eq('customer_id', refereeCustomerId)

   84:     })

   86:

   88: 
   89:   return { completed: true, referrerPoints: config.referrer_reward_points, refereePoints: config.referee_reward_points }
   90: }

codex
Two concrete risks are already confirmed. First, the current server client uses the Supabase service role, while Dutchie routes only require a session and trust an unsigned location override cookie. The plan’s “full stack audit” never audits authorization or tenant ownership. Second, the proposed 108,663 row loyalty sync runs through a Vercel route capped at 30 seconds, but the plan has no durable job or resumable execution model. I’m checking migration dependencies and whether the acceptance gates can actually detect these failures.

Effects are intended to synchronize state between React and external systems such as manually updating the DOM, state management libraries, or other platform APIs. In general, the body of an effect should do one or both of the following:
* Update external systems with the latest state from React.

Calling setState synchronously within an effect body causes cascading renders that can hurt performance, and is not recommended. (https://react.dev/learn/you-might-not-need-an-effect).

Effects are intended to synchronize state between React and external systems such as manually updating the DOM, state management libraries, or other platform APIs. In general, the body of an effect should do one or both of the following:

## Verified API facts (Sol: trust these over Swagger)

- Auth: `Authorization: Basic base64(apiKey + ':')`
- Transactions: `GET /reporting/transactions` â€” `FromDateUTC`/`ToDateUTC` (max 60-day window; chunk at 55), `IncludeDetail=true`, `IncludeTaxes=true`
- Customers: `GET /customer/customers-paginated` â€” `PageNumber`/`PageSize` (max 1000), supports `fromLastModifiedDateUTC`
- Products: `GET /products` â€” single request returns all; supports `fromLastModifiedDateUTC`
- Inventory: `GET /reporting/inventory` â€” `Skip`/`Take` (max 5000) (`/inventory` returns empty â€” do not use)
- Employees: `GET /employees` â€” fields are `userId`, `fullName`, `status`, `groups`
- Loyalty: `GET /reporting/loyalty-snapshot` â€” no params, returns ALL customers `[{customerId:int, loyaltyBalance:double, loyaltySpent:double, loyaltyEarned:double}]`, rate-limited 1/min, nightly-refreshed
- Supabase gotchas: 1000-row default limit (page with `.range()` in 1000 chunks); PostgREST upsert needs a real UNIQUE constraint; dedupe batch upserts by conflict key; `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'` after DDL.

## Phase A â€” Site-wide audit & fix (broken links, APIs, schemas, UI, edge cases)

Scale: 102 pages, 229 API routes, 84 components.

Method (Sol executes in this order, recording every finding in `.route/AUDIT.md` as `A-<n>: <file:line> â€” <problem> â€” <fix>`):

1. **Route inventory**: enumerate all `page.tsx` paths â†’ the set of real routes. Grep all `href=`, `router.push(`, `redirect(` targets in `src/` â†’ flag + fix any target not in the set (or dynamic targets whose base segment doesn't exist).
2. **API call inventory**: grep all `fetch('/api/...')` client calls â†’ verify each path has a matching `route.ts` exporting that HTTP method. Flag + fix mismatches, including response-shape mismatches (known bug class: pages reading `json.data` when routes return named keys).
3. **Schema conformance**: cross-check every `.insert(`/`.update(`/`.upsert(` payload against `DATABASE-CONSTRAINTS.md` CHECK constraints and NOT NULLs. Fix any value not in the allowed list. Known bug classes: invented enum values, missing org/location scoping.
4. **UI dead-ends**: buttons with no-op/missing handlers, forms whose submit hits a nonexistent endpoint, modals that can't close, `onClick` referencing undefined functions, HTML entity corruption (`&apos;` rendered literally), dropdowns clipped by `overflow-hidden` parents.
5. **Edge cases**: null `locationId` (all-locations mode) crashes, empty-array `.map` states with no empty-state UI on list pages, unguarded `.toFixed()`/date parses on nullable fields, division by zero in stats.
6. **Known open bug**: Dutchie settings page Sync History table shows `--` in DATE column â€” the log API/response field mapping is broken; fix so real timestamps render (US Mountain time).

Acceptance criteria:
- AC-A1: `.route/AUDIT.md` lists every finding with file:line and the applied fix; zero findings left in "found but unfixed" state (or explicitly justified as out-of-scope with reason).
- AC-A2: Every internal `href`/`router.push` target resolves to an existing route (verified by the inventory script output included in AUDIT.md).

- AC-A4: No DB write path uses enum values absent from DATABASE-CONSTRAINTS.md.
- AC-A5: Sync History DATE column renders real dates.
- AC-A6: No page crashes on null location selection (spot-fix any found).

## Phase B â€” Dutchie sync: hardening + loyalty points sync

B1. **Loyalty sync (new entity)** â€” schema facts VERIFIED on dev 2026-07-14:
- `loyalty_balances` columns: `current_points` INTEGER NOT NULL, `lifetime_points` INTEGER NOT NULL, `customer_id` UUID NOT NULL, `organization_id` UUID NOT NULL, `enrolled_at` TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL, `tier_id` nullable. UNIQUE `(customer_id, organization_id)` exists (upsert conflict key ready). `customers.dutchie_customer_id` INTEGER exists.
- Migration `2026xxxx_dutchie_loyalty_sync.sql`: (1) widen `loyalty_balances.current_points` and `lifetime_points` to `NUMERIC(12,2)` â€” Dutchie balances are decimals (live sample: 162.27) and INTEGER would silently truncate customer points; (2) add `sync_loyalty BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE` and `last_synced_loyalty_at TIMESTAMPTZ` to `dutchie_config`; (3) `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'`. Audit any code doing integer math on these columns.
- `syncEngine.ts`: new `syncLoyalty` â€” one snapshot call per location run; map `customerId` â†’ local customer via `customers.dutchie_customer_id` (batch the lookup in 1000-row pages); upsert `loyalty_balances` with `current_points = loyaltyBalance`, `lifetime_points = loyaltyEarned`, `enrolled_at` supplied on insert (now()), onConflict `customer_id,organization_id`, deduped 1000-row chunks; skip-and-count unmatched customerIds; update `last_synced_loyalty_at`.
- Rate limit: NEVER call the snapshot more than once per sync run; if `last_synced_loyalty_at` < 20h ago, still allow manual re-sync but log a freshness note (data refreshes nightly upstream).
- configLoader + types + `/api/dutchie/sync` VALID_ENTITY_TYPES + settings UI: add `loyalty` entity tile with its own sync button + timestamp, matching existing tiles.
- Fix the existing `syncTransactions` configKey mismatch (UI references a config field that doesn't exist in DutchieLocationConfig).

B2. **Sync engine quality pass**
- Incremental sync: entities supporting `fromLastModifiedDateUTC` (customers, products) must use it when a last-synced timestamp exists; transactions chunk 55-day windows; inventory pages Skip/Take.
- Single-flight guard: prevent two concurrent syncs for the same location+entity (in-memory lock is acceptable for single-instance dev; note Vercel multi-instance caveat in code comment).
- Error handling: per-record errors must not abort the batch; batch upserts deduped by conflict key; every path writes a complete `dutchie_sync_log` row (no orphaned 'running' rows â€” add a finally/catch that closes the log as failed).
- Performance: no per-record awaited queries in loops (batch lookups); BATCH_SIZE consistency.

Acceptance criteria:
- AC-B1: Loyalty entity syncs end-to-end on dev: snapshot fetched once, balances upserted, unmatched counted, timestamp updated, sync_log row complete. (Fable will live-verify against dev DB.)
- AC-B2: `loyalty` appears in settings UI with working per-entity sync + last-synced display.
- AC-B3: `syncTransactions` config mismatch fixed; all entity toggles round-trip (save â†’ reload â†’ persisted).
- AC-B4: Customers + products syncs use incremental `fromLastModifiedDateUTC` when available.
- AC-B5: No sync path can leave a `dutchie_sync_log` row stuck in 'running'.
- AC-B6: Concurrent duplicate sync for same location+entity is rejected with 409.

## Phase C â€” Universal theme system ("theme switch, not recode")

Architecture (Tailwind v4, already on `@theme inline`):
- `globals.css`: semantic token layer defined on `:root` (default = oasis-dark) and `[data-theme="oasis-light"]` (and future themes as new blocks ONLY). Tokens (CSS custom properties): 
  - Surfaces: `--bg`, `--surface`, `--surface-raised`, `--surface-overlay`
  - Borders: `--edge`, `--edge-strong`
  - Text: `--text-primary`, `--text-secondary`, `--text-muted`, `--text-inverse`
  - Brand: `--accent`, `--accent-hover`, `--accent-fg`, `--accent-soft`
  - Status: `--success`, `--warning`, `--danger`, `--info` + `-soft` surface variants
  - Charts: `--chart-1..6`; Focus: `--ring`; plus `--radius-*`, `--shadow-*`
- Map tokens via `@theme inline` to Tailwind utilities: `bg-surface`, `text-muted`, `border-edge`, `bg-accent`, etc.
- ThemeProvider: sets `data-theme` on `<html>`; persisted in cookie + localStorage; inline no-FOUC script in root layout; theme picker UI in Settings â†’ Appearance showing live preview swatches.
- Design language (from Mobbin refs â€” Supabase Studio calm-neutral dark + Lovable KPI cards): quieter borders, consistent radius, KPI stat cards with trend chips, refined table density. Applied by restyling SHARED components (DataTable, cards, buttons, inputs, modals, Sidebar, headers) â€” pages inherit.
- Codemod: replace hardcoded `gray-*`/`emerald-*`/`zinc-*` palette classes across all 144 affected files with semantic utilities. Charts read `--chart-*` vars.

Acceptance criteria:
- AC-C1: Zero hardcoded gray/emerald/zinc palette classes remain in `src/app` + `src/components` (grep gate = 0 matches, excluding globals.css itself).
- AC-C2: Switching theme in Settings instantly restyles terminal, backoffice, and storefront with no reload artifacts or FOUC on refresh.
- AC-C3: Adding a demo third theme (`oasis-contrast`, included) requires ONLY a new CSS block â€” no TSX changes. Its existence proves the contract.
- AC-C4: Default look remains dark+emerald; visual hierarchy per the design language above; WCAG AA contrast for text tokens in both shipped themes.
- AC-C5: Recharts components consume chart tokens (no hex literals in chart code).

## The Rule

**Invoke relevant or requested skills BEFORE any response or action** Ã¢â‚¬â€ including clarifying questions, exploring the codebase, or checking files. If it turns out wrong for the situation, you don't have to use it.

**Before entering plan mode:** if you haven't already brainstormed, invoke the brainstorming skill first.

Then announce "Using [skill] to [purpose]" and follow the skill exactly. If it has a checklist, create a todo per item.

## Skill Priority

When multiple skills apply, process skills come first Ã¢â‚¬â€ they set the approach, then implementation skills (frontend-design, etc.) carry it out. Brainstorming and systematic-debugging are Superpowers' most common process skills, but the rule holds for any of them.

- "Let's build X" Ã¢â€ â€™ superpowers:brainstorming first, then implementation skills.
- "Fix this bug" Ã¢â€ â€™ superpowers:systematic-debugging first, then domain skills.

## Red Flags

These thoughts mean STOPÃ¢â‚¬â€you're rationalizing:

| Thought | Reality |
|---------|---------|
| "This is just a simple question" | Questions are tasks. Check for skills. |
| "I need more context first" | Skill check comes BEFORE clarifying questions. |
| "Let me explore the codebase first" | Skills tell you HOW to explore. Check first. |
| "I can check git/files quickly" | Files lack conversation context. Check for skills. |
| "Let me gather information first" | Skills tell you HOW to gather information. |
| "This doesn't need a formal skill" | If a skill exists, use it. |
| "I remember this skill" | Skills evolve. Read current version. |
| "This doesn't count as a task" | Action = task. Check for skills. |
| "The skill is overkill" | Simple things become complex. Use it. |
| "I'll just do this one thing first" | Check BEFORE doing anything. |
| "This feels productive" | Undisciplined action wastes time. Skills prevent this. |
| "I know what that means" | Knowing the concept Ã¢â€°Â  using the skill. Invoke it. |

---
name: system-architect-auditor
description: >
  Veteran principal-level systems architect with 25+ years auditing production software. Specialty is forensic review of existing codebases on the Next.js / Supabase / PostgreSQL / Vercel stack (also fluent in Node, TypeScript, React, Edge Functions, Postgres tuning, RLS, queue systems, vector stores, Microsoft Graph, OAuth, OpenAI / Anthropic API integrations) to find bottlenecks, design flaws, technical debt, security exposure, scalability ceilings, observability gaps, and silent failure modes. Use this skill whenever the user asks for an end-to-end audit of an existing application, a code review at the system level, a performance review, a "why is this slow" investigation, a refactor plan, a scaling assessment, an architecture critique, a technical-debt inventory, a pre-acquisition diligence, a pre-launch readiness review, a post-incident root-cause review, or wants a senior architect to look at a project and pinpoint what should be done better. Trigger when the user mentions audit, architecture review, system review, bottleneck, performance, scalability, technical debt, refactor, "look at the whole thing", "find the issues", code review across an app, integration risk, data model review, API surface review, RLS audit, query plan, latency, observability, or Case Watch. Trigger even without those words when the user describes an existing system and wants honest senior-level engineering judgment about what is wrong with it.
